***пошлый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пошлый.html>по́шлый</a> (1168)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">пошьлъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pošĭlŭ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">ancient, primordial, former, usual</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пошлый.html>по́шлый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">póšlyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)пошле́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)пошле́й</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>vulgar</li>
<li>commonplace, trivial, banal, trite</li></ol>

***пощечина.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пощечина.html>пощёчина</a> (10165)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:щека.html>щека́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ščeká</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cheek</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ина</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ina</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пощечина.html>пощёчина</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">poščóčina</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пощечина.html>пощёчины</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пощечина.html>пощёчины</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пощечина.html>пощёчин</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>slap in the face, box on the ear</li></ol>

***пощупать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пощупать.html>пощу́пать</a> (8810)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:щупать.html>щу́пать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ščúpatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пощупать.html>пощу́пать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">poščúpatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:щупать.html>щу́пать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to feel, to touch; to grope</li>
<li>to probe</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:поэзия.html>поэ́зия</a> (3898)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">poezja</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">poetry</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поэзия.html>поэ́зия</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">poézija</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поэзия.html>поэ́зии</a></b>, <i>uncountable</i>) (<i>no plural</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>poetry</li>
<li>charm, elegance, romantic appeal of something
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:точность.html>то́чность</a> — <b><a href = vnd.unilang:поэзия.html>поэ́зия</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:наука.html>нау́ки</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Tóčnostʹ — <b>poézija</b> naúki.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Accuracy is the charm of science.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">poetry</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">стихотворство</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">stixotvorstvo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">стихотворчество</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">stixotvorčestvo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">версифика́ция</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">versifikácija</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (<i>pejorative</i>)</li></ul>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">charm, elegance, romantic appeal</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:романтика.html>романтика</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">romantika</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***поэтесса.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:поэтесса.html>поэте́сса</a> (17563)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поэтесса.html>поэте́сса</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">poetɛ́ssa</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поэтесса.html>поэте́ссы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поэтесса.html>поэте́ссы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поэтесса.html>поэте́сс</a></b>, <i>masculine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поэт.html>поэ́т</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>poetess, woman poet</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>Sometimes interpreted as not quite equal to the masculine <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поэт.html>поэ́т</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">poét</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Several famous female Russian poets, notably <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Anna_Akhmatova" class="extiw" title="w:Anna Akhmatova">Anna Akhmatova</a> and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marina_Tsvetaeva" class="extiw" title="w:Marina Tsvetaeva">Marina Tsvetaeva</a>, insisted on being called <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поэт.html>поэ́т</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">poét</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, and regarded the term <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поэтесса.html>поэте́сса</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">poetɛ́ssa</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> as insulting.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поэт.html>поэ́т</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">poét</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поэма.html>поэ́ма</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">poéma</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***пояс.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пояс.html>по́яс</a> (1835)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*pȍjāsъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пояс.html>по́яс</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pójas</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пояс.html>по́яса</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пояс.html>пояса́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пояс.html>поясо́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>belt, girdle, band, waistband, cummerbund</li>
<li>zone, region</li>
<li>flange, collar, hoop</li>
<li>boom (of an arch)</li></ol>

***пояснивший.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пояснить.html>поясни́вший</a> (2395)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пояс.html>по́яс</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pójas</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ни́ца</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-níca</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поясница.html>поясни́ца</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pojasníca</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поясница.html>поясни́цы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поясница.html>поясни́цы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поясница.html>поясни́ц</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:поясняемый.html>поясня́емый</a> (9571)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
